    SELECT TOP(@__p_0) [p].[Id], [p].[Approved], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CountInStorage], [p].[Description], [p].[Model], [p].[PackageId], [p].[PreviewImage], [p].[Rating], [p].[RetailPrice], [p].[Series], [p].[Title], [p].[Type], [p].[VendorCode], [p].[WarrantyMonth]

) AS [t]

""SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Approved], [t].[BrandId], [t].[CategoryId], [t].[CountInStorage], [t].[Description], [t].[Model], [t].[PackageId], [t].[PreviewImage], [t].[Rating], [t].[RetailPrice], [t].[Series], [t].[Title], [t].[Type], [t].[VendorCode], [t].[WarrantyMonth], [b].[Id], [b].[Country], [b].[Description], [b].[Name], [c].[Id], [c].[ParentCategoryId], [c].[PreviewImage], [c].[Title], [p0].[Id], [p0].[CountInPackage], [p0].[Volume], [p0].[Weight], [i].[Id], [i].[FilePath], [i].[ProductId], [p1].[Id], [p1].[ProductId], [p1].[Title], [p1].[Value], [c0].[Id], [c0].[Date], [c0].[DislikesTotal], [c0].[IsRemoved], [c0].[LikesTotal], [c0].[ParentId], [c0].[ProductId], [c0].[Raiting], [c0].[Text], [c0].[UserId]
FROM (
    SELECT TOP(@__p_0) [p].[Id], [p].[Approved], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CountInStorage], [p].[Description], [p].[Model], [p].[PackageId], [p].[PreviewImage], [p].[Rating], [p].[RetailPrice], [p].[Series], [p].[Title], [p].[Type], [p].[VendorCode], [p].[WarrantyMonth]

    ORDER BY [p].[Rating] DESC
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Brand] AS [b] ON [t].[BrandId] = [b].[Id]

LEFT JOIN [Packages] AS [p0] ON [t].[PackageId] = [p0].[Id]

LEFT JOIN [ProductCharacteristics] AS [p1] ON [t].[Id] = [p1].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN [Comments] AS [c0] ON [t].[Id] = [c0].[ProductId]
ORDER BY [t].[Rating] DESC, [t].[Id], [b].[Id], [c].[Id], [i].[Id], [p1].[Id], [c0].[Id]"
